 ### 39\. <a id="one-thirty-nine">lesson thiyty-nine Dont drop it(别摔了)<a/>

######单词精讲

>drop

    英 [drɒp]  美 [drɑp]
    vt. 滴；使降低；使终止；随口漏出
    vi. 下降；终止
    n. 滴；落下；空投；微量；滴剂
    [ 过去式 dropped或dropt 过去分词 dropped或dropt 现在分词 dropping ]

    1.v (失手)落下，掉下
    She dropped her knife and fork and hurried to answer the phone.
    她放下刀子和叉子急忙的去接电话.
    2 v.(使)
    滴下;滴落.
    Tears dropped from her face.眼泪从她的脸上滑下。
    3.v.(使)下降;降低.
    He dropped his voice.他降下他的声音。
    Yesterday the temperature dropped to 8 below zero.


>tear

    英 [(for v.) ˈtɛː; (for n.) ˈtɪə]  美 [(for v.) ˈter; (for n.) ˈtir]
    n. 眼泪, （撕破的）洞或裂缝, 撕扯
    vt. 撕掉, 扯下, 扰乱
    vi. 流泪, 撕破
    n. (Tear)人名；(英)蒂尔

>front

    英 [frʌnt]  美 [frʌnt]
    n. 前面；正面；前线
    vt. 面对；朝向；对付
    vi. 朝向
    adj. 前面的；正面的
    adv. 在前面；向前
    n. (Front)人名；(法)弗龙
    front line 前线

    in front of 在...前面 (属于不同范围)
    There is a gardon in front of the building.
    有一个花园的在这个建筑前面。花园和建筑不属于同一范围。
    in the front of     (属于同一范围)
    There is blackborad in the front of the classroom.
    在教室的前面有一个黑板。黑板在教室的里面。属于同一范围。



>careful

    英 [ˈkeəfl]  美 ['kɛrfl]
    adj. 仔细的，小心的
    [ 比较级 more careful 最高级 most careful ]
    Be careful!小心点！
    Look out!小心点！

>careless

    英 ['keələs]  美 ['kɛrləs]
    adj. 粗心的；无忧无虑的；淡漠的
    n. (Careless)人名；(英)凯尔利斯
    [ 比较级 more careless 最高级 most careless ]

>care

    英 [keə]  美 [kɛr]
    n. 照料；关怀；忧虑；谨慎
    vi. 照顾；关心；顾虑；喜爱
    vt. 在意；希望或喜欢

    n. (Care)人名；(英)凯尔；(塞)察蕾
    [ 过去式 cared 过去分词 cared 现在分词 caring ]
    take care of.... 照顾好....
    look after....照顾好....
    You must take care of/look after her. 你必须照顾好她.
    Jim is sick,I have to take care of/look after him.吉姆生病了,我必须照顾好他.
    I don't care.我不在乎。
    Who cares?谁关心/在乎呢？

>sick

       英 [sɪk]  美 [sɪk]
       adj. 厌恶的；病态的；不舒服；渴望的；恶心的 ；生病的
       n. 病人
       n. (Sick)人名；(德、西)西克
       vt. 使狗去咬；呕吐；追击

>vase

    英 [vɑːz]  美 [veɪs; veɪz]
    n. 瓶；花瓶
    n. (Vase)人名；(塞、罗、芬)瓦塞

>flower

    英 ['flaʊə]  美 ['flaʊɚ]
    n. 花；精华；开花植物
    vi. 成熟，发育；开花；繁荣；旺盛
    vt. 使开花；用花装饰
    n. (Flower)人名；(英)弗劳尔


###### 语法精讲

>祈使句

    祈使句句型形式
    1.普通动词原形+其它(名词或代词)
    Help yourself!随意！
    Keep off the grass.请勿践踏草地。
    2.be动词+形容词
    Be careful!小心点.
    Be quite!安静点!

    祈使句的否定形式 Don't=Do not
    祈使句的否定形式，就是在祈使句句首加一个Don't
    Put on your coat.穿上你的大衣 -否定形式->Don't put on your coat.不要穿上你的大衣。
    Give him a knife.--->Don't give him a knife.
    Be careful. 小心点--->Don't be careful.不要小心。

###### 课文录音
      Listen thirty nine.
      Don't drop it.
      Listen to the table,then answer the questions.

      What are you going to do with that vase,Penny?
        do with ...处理...
      I'm going to put it on this table,Sam.
      Don't do that.Give it to me.
      不要那样做，把他给我.
      What are you going to do with it?
      I'm going to put it here,in fornt of the window.
      Be careful,Don't drop it!
      Don't put it here,Sam.Put it here,on this shelf.
      There we are!It's a lovely vase.
      Those flowers are lovely,too.

     What am I going to do with your mistake?
     我将要如何处理你的错误呢？
     What am I going to do with my work?
     我将如何处理我的工作呢？

     with:和...,与...在一起.随着，用。支持、
     I am with you .我和你在一起。
     She came to  the park with a dog.

     Don't do that.Give it to me.
     do that 对应上文的put it on this tabel.->Don't put it on this table.
     换成祈使句的否定形式 Don't do that.表示不要做上面的那件事，不要那样做。
     不要那样做，把他给我.

     Thare we are!口语 表示放好了.

######口语快门

        如何在照相的时候说一些有意思的话.

        照相比较正式的说法是
        take pictures.
        Let's take a picture.
        Let's get the picture taken.
        美语口语中用的多的是
        Pictures time!照相时间! ==photo time!

        Could you take a picture for me?
        你能为我照一个相片吗？

         Say cheese.说奶酪.表示笑一下。(就表示中国里的茄子的意思)
         The camera(相机) likes me.相机喜欢我。就表示我很上镜的意思.
         The camera likes you.你很上镜.
         I want to develop my photos.原意是我想去发展我的照片.就表示我想去冲我的照片.
         I want to make a photo album(相册).我想去做一个相片册。

        album
        英 ['ælbəm]  美 ['ælbəm]
        n. 相簿；唱片集；集邮簿；签名纪念册

###### 歌词欣赏

        Justin Bieber
        Baby

### 40\. <a id="one-forty">lesson forty  What are you going to do?<a/>

###### 单词精讲

>show

    英 [ʃəʊ]  美 [ʃo]
    vt. 显示；说明；展出；演出
    vi. 显示；说明；指示
    n. 显示；表演；炫耀
    n. (Show)人名；(中)邵(普通话·威妥玛)；(英)肖
    [ 过去式 showed 过去分词 showed 或 shown 现在分词 showing ]
    1 .给....看
    show sth. to sb.. 把某物展示给某人看
    I want to show the picture to him.我想把照片给他看。
    I want to show him the picture.
    2.n. 表演
    It is a great show.它是一个很棒的表演。

>send

    英 [send]  美 [sɛnd]
    vt. 发送，寄；派遣；使进入；发射
    vi. 派人；寄信
    n. 上升运动
    n. (Send)人名；(德)森德
    [ 过去式 sent 过去分词 sent 现在分词 sending ]

    send a letter.送一封信.
    send sb.sth/send sth.to sb. 送某人某物
    I want to send her a flower.我想去送她一个花。

>take

     [teɪk]  美 [tek]
    vt. 拿，取；采取；接受（礼物等）；买，花费；耗费,带给（时间等）
    vi. 拿；获得
    n. 捕获量；看法；利益，盈益；（入场券的）售得金额

    1.带给
    I am going to take him some books.我将要带给他一些书.

###### 听录音
    Listen forty
    Do know open your book?
    Listen.
    Do know speak?

    Are you going to put on your hat?
    Yes,I'm going to  put it on.

    What are you going to do?
    I am going to take it off.

    What are you going to do ?
    I am going turn it off.

     Whata are you going to do ?
     I am going to turn it on.



    动词词组: 动词+介词 动词短语加名词或代词的不同形式
    动词+介词+名词/动词+名词+介词
    (动词+介词构成的动词短语 加名词可以放在介词之后，也可以放在动词和介词之间)
    Put on your coat!=Put your coat on!
    Take off your coat!=Take your coat off!
    动词+代词+介词 （动词+介词构成的动词短语时，加代词，必须放到动词和介词之间）

    What are you going to do with that/those...?
    do with 处理
    I'm going to give/show/send/take...

    What are you  going to do with that dress?
    I'm going to give it to my daughter.

    What are you going to do with those flowers?
    I am going to send them to my grandmother.

    What are you going to do with that newspaper?
    I am going to show it to my father.

    What are you going to do with that picture?
    I am going to take it to my mother.

    What are you going to do with those ice cream?
    I am going to take them to the children.

    What are you going to do with those flowers?
    I am going to send them to my wife.

    What are you going to do with that letter?
    I am going to send it to my grandfather.

    What are you going to do with those books?
    I am going to give them to my sister.

######书面练习

     A Rwrite these sentences.
     模仿例句改写一下句子。
     Give me that vase.
     Give sb sth/Give sth to sb.

     1.Send George that letter.
     Send thar letter to George.

     2.Take her those flowers.
       Take those flowers to her.

     3.Show me that picture.
      Show that picture to me .

     4.Give Mrs.Jones these books.
      Give these books to Mrs.Jones.

     5.Give the children these ice creams.
       Give these ice creams to the children.

     B Rwrite these sentences.
     Put on your coat!
     I'm going to put it on！

     Put on your shoes!
     I'm going to put them on!

     Put on your hat!
     I'm going to put it on!

     Take off your shoes!
     I'm going to take them off .

     Turn on the taps!
     I'm going to turn them on.

     Turn off the light!
     I'm going to turn  it off.

     Put on your suit!
     I'm going to put it on.

     Take off your hat!
     I'm going to take it off.

     Turn on the lights!
     I'm going to turn them on.

     Turn off the television.
     I'm going to turn it off.

     Turn off the lights!
     I'm going to turn them off.

     Turn on the stereo.
     I'm going to turn it on.

######课文录音
    Penny's bag

    Is that bag heavy,penny?
    Not very.
    Here!
    Put it on this chair!
    What's in it?
    A piece of cheese.
    A loaf of bread.
    A bar of soap.
    A bar of chocolate.
    A bottle of milk.
    A pound of sugar.
    Half a pound of coffee.
    A quarter of a pound of tea.
    And a tin of tobacco.
    Is that tin of tobacco for me ?
    Well,it's certainly not for me!

    文章解析 ：
    不可数名词的数量： a+量词+不可数名词


###### 口语快门
    如何说我累了

    Tired:疲劳的
    I'm tired!

    精疲力竭的
    exhausted
    英 [ɪɡ'zɔːstɪd]  美 [ɪɡ'zɔstɪd]
    adj. 疲惫的；耗尽的
    v. 耗尽；用尽；使…精疲力尽（exhaust的过去式）
    I am exhausted.我是精疲力竭的。

    英文中也有累的跟狗一样的词
    dog-tired:累的跟狗一样
    I am dog-tired.就表示 我累的跟狗一样。

    累的时候说我需要休息一会
    需要：need to ..
    放松 :relax

    relax
    英 [rɪ'læks]  美 [rɪ'læks]
    vi. 放松，休息；松懈，松弛；变从容；休养
    vt. 放松；使休息；使松弛；缓和；使松懈

    I need to relax.为需要去休息。

    Take a rest .休息一下.（短语）
    I need to take a rest.我需要去休息一下.

### 42\. <a id="one-forty-two">lesson forty-two Is there a ... in/on that?<a/>

######单词精讲



######听录音

    Loook number thirty
    Is there a passport here?

###### 书面练习
     A Complete these sentences using a ,any and some.
     完成以下句子，用a,any,or some 填空
     There's a photograph on the desk.

     Is there any milk in the bottle?
     There isn't any milk in the bottle.
     There is some milk in that cup.

     1. Is there _any _ bread in the kitchen?
     2.There is _a_ loag on the table.
     3.There is _some_ coffee on the table,too.
     4.There isn't _any_ chocolate on the table.
     5.There is _a_ spoon on that dish.
     6.Is there _any_ soap on the dressing table?

    B. Write questions and answers using these words.
    模仿例句提问并回答.
    Examples:
    passport/on the table
    Is there a passport here?
    Yes,there is.
    There is one on the table.

    Bread/on the table.
    Is there any bread here?
    Yes.there is.
    There are some on the table.

    1.spoon/on the plate
    Is there a spoon here?
    Yes,there is.
    There is a spoon on the plate.

    2.tie/on the chair
    Is there a tie here?
    Yes,there is.
    There is one on the chdair.

    3.milk/on the table
    Is there any milk here?
    Yes,there is.
    There is some on the table.

    4.hammer/on the bookcase
    Is there a hammer here?
    Yes,there is.
    There is one on the bookcase.

    five.tea/on the table.
    Is there any tea here?
    Yes,there is.
    There is some on the table.

    six.vase/on the radio
    Is there a vase here?
    Yes,there is.
    There is one on the radio.

    seven. suit/in the wordrobe
    Is there a suit here?
    Yes,there is.
    There is one in the wordrobe.

    eight.tobacco/in the tin
    Is there any tobacco here?
    Yes,there is.
    There is some in the tin.

    nine.chocolate/on the desk
    Is there any chocolate here?
    Yes,there is.
    There is some on the desk.

    ten.chess/on the plate
    Is there any chess here?
    Yes,there is.
    There is some on the plate.

### 43\. <a id="one-forty-three">lesson forty-three Hurry up!<a/>

######单词精讲

>of course

    当然

>of course not

    当然不

    做当然的意思的时候口语中有多个词可以表达
    certainly(口语和书面语)
    sure(美语用的比较多)
    absolutely


>kettle

    英 ['ket(ə)l]  美 ['kɛtl]
    n. 壶；[化工] 釜；罐；鼓;水壶
    n. (Kettle)人名；(英)凯特尔

>behind

    英 [bɪ'haɪnd]  美 [bɪ'haɪnd]
    prep. 落后于；晚于;支持；在...后面
    adv. 在后地；在原处
    n. 屁股
     I am behind you.我在你身后.(我支持你.)

>teapot

    英 ['tiːpɒt]  美 ['ti'pɑt]
    n. 茶壶
    小题大做

>now

    英 [naʊ]  美 [naʊ]
    adv. 现在；如今；立刻
    adj. 现在的
    n. 现在；目前
    conj. 由于；既然

>find

    英 [faɪnd]  美 [faɪnd]
    vt. 查找，找到；发现；认为；感到；获得
    vi. 裁决
    n. 发现
    n. (Find)人名；(丹)芬
    1. v. 找到;寻得;
    It is hard to find a good person for the job.
    2.v.找出;查明
    Can we find an answer to the tough problem?

>flag

    英 [flæg]  美 [flæg]
    vi. 标记；衰退；枯萎
    vt. 标记；插旗
    n. 标志；旗子
    [ 过去式 flagged 过去分词 flagged 现在分词 flagging ]

>boil

    英 [bɒɪl]  美 [bɔɪl]
    vi. 煮沸；沸腾；激动，激昂；
    vt. 煮沸，烧开；使…激动；使…蒸发
    n. 沸腾，煮沸；疖子
    n. (Boil)人名；(俄)博伊尔
    1.v 开，滚，沸腾.

    2.v(海水等)翻腾;汹涌
    The stormy sea is boiling.暴风雨的海水是翻腾了。
    3.v(人的情绪)激动;发怒。
    See the notional flag made me boil.看着国旗使我激动.

######肯问录音

    Can you make the tea,Sam?
    Yes,of course I can,Penny.
    Is there any water in this kettle?
    Yes,there is.
    Where's the tea?
    It's over there,behind the teapot.
    Can you see it?
    I can see the teapot,but I can't see the tea.
    There it is! It's in front of you!

    Ah yes!I can see it now.
    Where are the cups?
    There are some in the cupboard.
    Can you find them?
    Yes,Here they are.
    Hurry up,Sam!The kettle's boiling!
    文章解析

    Can you make the tea,Sam?
    make the tea;沏茶
    make 用法
    1.v. 制作;创造
    Hollywood(好莱坞) can make the most famous film stars in the world.好莱坞会创造世界最著名的电影明星.
    2.v.产生，引起;导致
    You have made a serious mistake.你导致一个严重的错误。
    Don't make so much noise,please!请不要引起如此多的噪音！
    3.v.整理;料理;准备;
    The coffee is made.一杯咖啡被准备
    I am making a cup of coffee我正在准备一杯咖啡。

######语法精讲

    情态动词can的用法
    can 是情态动词,必须与其他动词连用,没有人称和数个的变化。
    can的否定形式为can't和cannot.
    I can make the tea.我可以沏杯茶。
    I can't make the tea.我不可以沏杯茶 。
    Can you make the tea?你可以沏杯茶吗？
    Yes,I can./No,I can't.是的，我可以。/不，我不可以/
    What can you do?你可能做什么？

    我可以画画
    I can paint.
    I can't paint.
    Can you paint?
    Yes,I can./No,I can't.
    What can you do?你可以做什么？

    我可以踢足球。
    I can play football.
    I can't play football.
    Can you play football?
    Yes,I can./No,I can't.
    What can you do?

    她可以唱很多的歌曲
    She can sing songs.
    She can't sing songs.
    Can She sing songs?
    Yes,she can./No,she can't.
    What can she do?

    他们可以去游泳
    They can go swimming.
    Can they go swimming?
    Yes,They can./No,They can't.
    What can they do?

    凯西可以来我的派对
    Cathy can come to my party.
    Cathy can't come to my party.
    Can Cathy come to my party?
    Yes,She can./No,She can't.
    What Can Cathy do?

######歌词欣赏

        LENKA
      Trouble is a Friend

### 44\. <a id="one-forty-four">lesson forty-four Are there ayn..?Is there any ...?<a/>

    Are there any....?后面接可数名词复数
    Is there any....?后面接不可数名词

###### 听录音
    repetition drill

    There is some on the table.

    look number eighty
    Are there any hammers here?

    There is some on the cupboard.

    Are there any newspapers here?

     look number four hundred

      Look number ninety hundred
      Is there any coffee here?
      Yes,there is.
      There is some on the table.

###### 书面练习

    复习：名词的复数形式
     1.通常在词尾加s
     friend-friends
     cat-cats
     sport-sports
     2.以s,x,z,ch,sh结尾的词在词尾加es
     glass--glasses
     bus-buses
     fox-foxes
     trash-trashes
     3.以y结尾的名词，以辅音字母+y结尾，先变y为i再加es.
     candy-candies
     lady--ladies
     4.以f或fe结尾的名词,把f或fe变为v再加es.
     wife--wives
     leaf---leaves
     5.以o结尾的名词加es.
     tomato-tomatoes
     potato--potatoes
     6.有一些名词原形和复数形式没有变化。(表示动物的名词单复数同形)
      fish
      sheep
      cattle
     7.一些名词的复数形式变化不规则
     man-men
     woman-women
     chlid-children
     person-people

     A.Write these sentences.
     改写一下句子，用名词的复数形式填空.
     Example:
     I can see some cups
     But I can't see any _galsses_.

     1.I can see some spoons,
     But I can't see any _knives_.

     2.I can see some hammers,
       but I can't see any boxes.

      3.I can see some coffee,
       but I can't see any loaves of bread.

      4.I can see some cupboards,
        but I can't see any shelves.

      five.I can see Mr.Jones and Mr.Brown.
      but I can't see their wives.

      six. I can see some cups,
      but I can't see any dishes.

      seven.I can see some cars,
        but I can't see any buses.

      B.Write questions and answers using these words.
       模仿例句提问并回答.
       Example:bread/on the table
       Is there any bread here?
       Yes,there is.There's some on the table.

       hammers/behind that box
       Are there any hammers here?
       Yes,there are.There are some behind that box.

        1.milk/ in front of the door.
        Is there any milk here?
        Yes,there is.
        There is some in front of the door.

        2.soap on the cupboard
        Is there any soap here?
        Yes,there is.
        There is some on the cupboard.

        3.newspapers behind that vase
        Are there any newspapers here?
        Yes,there are.
        There are some behind that vase.

        4.water in those galsses
        Is there any water here?
        Yes,there is.
        There is some in those galsses.

        5.tea in those cups
        Is there any tea here?
        Yes,there is.
        There is some in those cups.

        6.cups in front of that kettle.
        Are there any cups here?
        Yes,there are.
        There are some in front of that kettle.

        7.chocolate behind that book
        Is there any chocolate here?
        Yes,there is.
        There is some behind that book.

        8.teapots in the cupboard.
         Are there any teapots here?
         Yes,there are.
         There are some in the cupboard.

        Yes,there are.
        There are some in front of that building.

        10.coffee on the table

#######口语快门

        与can't相关的句型

           I can't hear myself think.我不可能听见我自己的想法了.(言外之意叫别人安静点)

           I can't help it.我忍不住了()
           (例如：发工资了，自己忍不住要去买很多东西。我忍不住了，就可以用I can't help it.)

### 45\. <a id="one-forty-five">lesson  forty-five The boss's letter<a/>

######单词精讲

>can

    英 [kæn]  美 [kæn]
    vt. 将…装入密封罐中保存
    aux. 能； 能够； 可以； 可能
    n. 罐头； （用金属或塑料制作的）容器； （马口铁或其他金属制作的）食品罐头
    I can speak English.情态动词句子结构
    I can't speak English.
    Yes,I can./No,I can't.
    What can you do?


>boss

    boss
    英 [bɒs]  美 [bɑs]
    n. 老板；首领；工头
    vt. 指挥，调遣；当…的领导
    vi. 当首领，发号施令
    n. (Boss)人名；(英、法、德、西、瑞典)博斯
    [ 第三人称单数 bosses 过去式 bossed 过去分词 bossed 现在分词 bossing ]
    He is very bossy().他是非常指挥会他人的.
    boss sb around.使唤某人.
    My boss   me around every day.我的老板每天都使唤我.

>bossy

    英 ['bɒsɪ]  美 ['bɔsi]
    adj. 专横的；浮雕装饰的；爱指挥他人的
    n. 母牛；牛犊
    n. (Bossy)人名；(法、罗)博西
    [ 比较级 bossier 最高级 bossiest ]

>minute

    英 ['mɪnɪt]  美 ['mɪnɪt]
    n. 分，分钟；片刻，一会儿；备忘录，笔记；会议记录
    vt. 将…记录下来
    adj. 微小的，详细的 [maɪˈnjuːt; US -ˈnuːt; maɪˋnut]
    wait for sb。（等待某人,表示长时间等待） I am waiting for you.我正在等待你
    a minute/one minute.(表示短暂的等待) 等待一分钟。.
    a second/one second

>ask

    英 [ɑːsk]  美 [æsk]
    vt. 问，询问；要求；需要；邀请；讨价
    vi. 问，询问；要求
    n. (Ask)人名；(芬、瑞典)阿斯克
    I want to ask a question.我想询问一个问题。
    I need to ask her phone number.
    I need to ask my friend.

>handwriting

    英 ['hændraɪtɪŋ]  美 ['hænd'raɪtɪŋ]
    n. 笔迹；书法；书写；手稿
    v. 亲手写（handwrite的ing形式）
    His handwriting is very neat.他的书写是非常整洁的。
    His handwriting is very messy.他的书写是非常糟糕的.

>terrible

    英 [ˈterəbl]  美 ['tɛrəbl]
    adj. 可怕的；很糟的；令人讨厌的
    adv. 很，非常
    [ 比较级 more terrible 最高级 most terrible ]

    1.adj, 可怕的，糟糕的
    Chinese football is terrible.
    2adj. 困难的；费劲的
    This is a terrible.
    3.极度的；非常严重的。
    I 've got a terrible headache.
    我有一个非常严重的头疼.
    4.糟糕的(口语)；很蹩脚的.
    She is terrible at maths.
    他的数学很蹩脚。

     [ 过去式 preferred 过去分词 preferred 现在分词 preferring ]

### 46\. <a id="one-forty-six">lesson  forty-six Can you...?<a/>

######单词精讲

>lift

    英 [lɪft]  美 [lɪft]
    vt. 举起；提升；鼓舞；空运；抄袭
    vi. 消散；升起；耸立
    n. 电梯；举起；起重机；搭车
    I can lift this table.我可以举起这张桌子.
    He can't lift that chair.他不能举起那张椅子。

>biscuit

    英 ['bɪskɪt]  美 ['bɪskɪt]
    n. 小点心，饼干
    [ 复数 biscuits ]


>cake

     英 [keɪk]  美 [kek]
     n. 蛋糕；块状物；利益总额
     vt. 使结块
     vi. 结成块状
     n. (Cake)人名；(英)凯克；(塞)察凯
     [ 过去式 caked 过去分词 caked 现在分词 caking ]


######听录音

    look number one  thousand.
     (Can you put your hat on?)
    I can put my hat on,but I can't put my coat on.
    look number five thousand.
    (Can you see that areoplane?)
    I can see that areoplane,but I can't see a bird.
    look number ten thousand.
    (Can you panit this bookcase?)
    I can paint this bookcase,but I can't paint this room.
    Look  number one hundred thousand.
    (Can you lift that chair?)
    I can lift that chair,but I can't lift this table.
    Look  number two hundred  and ten  thousand.
    (Can you read this book？)
    I can read this book,but I can't  read this magazine.
    Look  number three hundred fifty  thousand.
    (Can you jump off this box?)
    I can jump off this box.but I can't jump off that wall.
    Look  number five hundred thousand.
     (Can you make cakes? )
    I can make cakes,but I can't make biscuits.
    Look  number one million.
    (Can you put the vase on the table? )
    I can put the vase on the table.but I can't put it on the shlef.

###### 书面练习
    模仿例句改写以下句子
    Example:
    He is taking his book. He can take his book.
    She is putting on her coar.She can put on her coat.

    1.They are typing these letters.
      They can type these letters.

    2. She ie making the bed.
       She can make the bed.

    3.You are swimming across the river.
      You can swim arcoss the river.

    4.We are coming now.
      We can come now.

    5.We are running across the park.
      We can running across the park.

    6.He is sitting on the grass.
      He can sit on the grass.

    7.I am giving him some chocolate.
     I can give him some chocolate.

    B.Write questions and answers using I,he,she,it,we or they/
      模仿例句写出相应的对话，选用I,he,she,,it,we,they等代词
      Examples:
      Can you put on your coat?
      Yes,I can.
      What can you do?
      I can put on my coat.

     Can you and Sam listen to the radio?
     Yes,we can.
     What can you and Sam do?
     We can listen to the radio.

     1.Can you type this letter?
     Yes,I can.
     What can you do?
     I can type this letter.

     2. Can Penny wait for the bus?
        Yes,She can.
        What can She do?
        She can wait for the bus.

     3.Can Penny and Jane wash the dishes?
     Yes,They can.
     What can they do?
     They can wash the dishes.

     4.Can George take these flowers to her?
     Yes,he can.
     What can he do?
     He can take these flowers to her.

     5.Can the cat drink its milk?
     Yes,it can.
     What can it do?
     It can drink its milk.

     6.Can you and Sam paint this bookcase?
     Yes,We can.
     What can  you and Sam do?
     We can paint this bookcase.

     7.Can you see that areoplane.
     Yes,I can.
     What can you do?
     I can see that areoplane.

     8.Can Jane read this book?
     Yes,she can.
     What can she do ?
     She can read this book.

### 47\. <a id="one-forty-seven">lesson forty-seven A cup of coffee<a/>

###### 单词精讲

>like

    英 [laɪk]  美 [laɪk]
    vt. 喜欢；想；愿意
    vi. 喜欢；希望
    prep. 像；如同
    adj. 同样的；相似的
    n. 爱好；同样的人或物
    adv. 可能
    conj. 好像
    [ 过去式 liked 过去分词 liked 现在分词 liking ]

>want

    英 [wɒnt]  美 [wɔ:nt; wɔnt]
    vt. 需要；希望；应该；缺少
    n. 需要；缺乏；贫困；必需品
    vi. 需要；缺少

及物动词 ：动词后面可加名词

    like  want

     I like movies. 我喜欢电影
     I like cats.我喜欢猫
     I want her.我想她
     I want a cup of coffee.我想要一杯咖啡
      like和come 都构成动词短语
     like to .. 喜欢..
     want to ...  想要...
     I like to go swimming.我喜欢去游泳.
     I want to go shopping.
不及物动词: 动词后面不可以直接加名词

    come    go
    come
    The cars are coming out of the building.
     这些汽车正在从大楼里出来.
    go
    The cars are going into the building.
    这些汽车正在进入这个大楼.


###### 课文录音

    Do you like coffee,Ann?
    Yes,I do.
    Do you want a cup?
    Yes,please,Christine.
    Do you want any sugar?
    Yes,please.
    Do you want any milk?
    No,thank you.I don't like milk in my coffee.
    I like black coffee.
    Do you like biscuits?
    Yes,I do.
    Do you want one?
    Yes,I please.

    语法精讲
    一般现在时定义
    1.经常的习惯或反复的动作.
    He is lazy.
    2.现在的事实或状态描述
    I want a bike.
    一般现在的句式
    1.肯定句式
    be动词根据主语不同的人称有不同的形式:
    I+am
    we/you/they+are
    he/she/it+is

    Shi is a worker.她是一个工人.
    They are workers.她们是工人.
    He is a student.他是一个学生.
    This is a book.这是一本书.
    There is a book.在那有一本书.

    动词(表示一个具体的的动作)
    I work.我工作.
    We drink coffe.我们喝咖啡.

    2.一般现在时的肯定句式变为疑问句式
     一般在句首加上助动词do来构成。
     do是对第一人称I或是人称的复数,I,you ,We,They...这样的主语的时候，
     在句首加上助动词do来构成疑问句的句式.
     动词一概不变，用原形.
     I work.
     Do I wrok?
     Yes,I do./No,I don't.
     We drink coffee.
     Do we drink coffee?
     Yes,We do./No,We don't.

     3.一般现在时的否定句式. 就是在陈述句的do后面加上Not或者是直接加上don't.
     I want a car.我想要一辆车
     否定句式：I don't want a car.我不想要一辆车。
     一般疑问句:do you want a car?你想要一辆汽车吗?
     回答: 肯定：Yes,I do.否定：No,I don't.
     特殊疑问句:what do you want? 你想要什么？

     I like moives.
     否定：I don't like movies.
     疑问: do you like movies?
     回答：Yes,I do./No,I don't.
     特殊疑问句;what do you like?

     We want to take a plane.
     We don't want to take a plane.
     Do you want to take a plane?
     Yes,We do./No,We don't.
     What do you want to do?

     we like to drink some coffee.
     we don't like to drink some coffee.
     Do you like to drink some coffee?
     Yes,We do./No,We don't.
     What do you like to do?

###### 书面练习

     1.I want some biscuits.
     I don't want some biscuits.
     Do you want sme biscuits?
     Yes.I do./No,I don't.
     What do you want?

     2.I like reading newspapers.
     I don't like reading newspapers.
     Do you like reading newspapers?
     Yes,I do./No,I don't.
     What do you like?

     3.You want money.
     You don't want money.
     Do you want money?
     Yes,you do./No,you don't.
     What do you want?

     4.We want to take a trip.
      We don't want to take a trip.
      Do you want to take a trip?
      Yes,We do./No,We don't.
      What do you want to do?

     5.We like to listen to some music.
      We don't like to listen to any music.
      Do you like to listen to some music?
      Yes,We do./No,we don't.
      What do you like to do?

###### 口语快门
    表示加油的词

     Way to go！加油！(也有祝贺你的意思)
     Go for it.加油！
     Come on!太棒了,加油,等！(在不同的语境有不同的意思)

    Sarah Brightmen
    Scarborough Fair

### 48\. <a id="one-forty-eight">lesson  forty-eight Do you like...?Do you want...?<a/>

    不可数名词要表示数量时，前面要加上表示数量的词修饰
    a bottle of wter 一瓶水
    b bar of bread 一条面包
    a loaf of soap 一块肥皂

###### 语法精讲
>序数词

>first

    英 [fɜːst]  美 [fɝst]

    英 [twelfθ]  美 [twɛlfθ]

    n. 第十二；月的第十二日

   序数词必须与定冠词the连用
    the first month 第一个月
    the twelfth century 第十二个世纪

### 49\. <a id="one-forty-nine">lesson  forty-nine At the butcher's<a/>

######单词精讲

>butcher

    英 [ˈbʊtʃə(r)]  美 [ˈbʊtʃər]
    vt. 屠杀
    n. 屠夫
    n. (Butcher)人名；(英)布彻

    在英语中表示“某一商店”的商店中，shop可省略.
     the butcher's(shop)
     the hairdresser's(shop)
     the doctor's(office)
     my mother's(house)
     这些词的后面表示某一人的商店或是建筑中的词都可省略.

>beef

     英 [biːf]  美 [bif]
     n. 牛肉；肌肉；食用牛；牢骚
     vi. 抱怨，告发；发牢骚
     vt. 养；加强
     [ 复数 beeves或beefs ]

>lamb

    英 [læm]  美 [læm]
    n. 羔羊，小羊；羔羊肉
    vt. 生小羊，产羔羊
    vi. 生小羊，产羔羊
    n. (Lamb)人名；(英)兰姆；(德)兰布

>pork

    英 [pɔːk]  美 [pɔrk]
    n. 猪肉
    vt. 与女子性交
    n. (Pork)人名；(俄)波尔克
    [ 过去式 porked 过去分词 porked 现在分词 porking ]

>steak

    英 [steɪk]  美 [stek]
    n. 牛排；肉排；鱼排
    pork steak 猪排
    lamb steak 羊排
    fis steak 鱼排

>mince

    英 [mɪns]  美 [mɪns]
    vt. 切碎；矫揉做作地说
    vi. 装腔作势；碎步走
    n. 切碎物，肉馅

>chicken

    英 ['tʃɪkɪn]  美 [ˈtʃɪkɪn]
    n. 鸡肉；小鸡；胆小鬼，懦夫
    adj. 鸡肉的；胆怯的；幼小的
    You are a chicken.你是一个胆小鬼.


>truth

    英 [truːθ]  美 [trʊθ]
    n. 真理；事实；诚实；实质
    [ 复数 truths ]

>true

    英 [truː]  美 [tru]
    adj. 真实的；正确的
    adv. 真实地；准确地
    n. 真实；准确
    vt. 装准
    n. (TRUE)人名；(英)特鲁
    [ 比较级 truer 最高级 truest 过去式 trued 过去分词 trued 现在分词 truing或trueing ]

>tell

    英 [tel]
    vt. 告诉，说；辨别；吩咐；断定
    vi. 讲述；告发，泄密；识别
    n. (Tell)人名；(英、德、瑞典)特尔；(罗、意)泰尔；(阿拉伯)塔勒
    [ 过去式 told 过去分词 told 现在分词 telling ]
    短语
    tell the truth 说实话
    tell a lie 撒谎
    tell a story 讲故事

>either

     英 ['aɪðə; 'iː-]  美 ['iðɚ]
     adj. 两者之中任一的；两者之中每一的
     prep. 任何一个
     conj. 也（用于否定句或否定词组后）；根本
     pron. 任一，两方，随便哪一个；两者中的一个或另一个
     也
     either 一般用于否定句，位于句末,前面通常有逗号.
     too 常用语肯定句，有时也用于疑问句，但不能用于否定句.
     - - I don't like this movie.我不喜欢这个电影。
     - -I don't like it,either.我也不喜欢这个电影。

######语法精讲
    一般现在时变为疑问句时，当是第一,二人称或是第三人称的复数时在句首加do。是第三人称单数时在句首加does.
    一般现在时变为疑问句时，在句首加上助动词do或does的方式构成，第三人称单数时用does,其余都用do.
    I like the cake.
    Do you like cake?
    Yes,I do./No,I don't.


    He likes the cake.
    Does he like the cake?
    Yes,he does./No,He does not.
    动词加s(es)规则.
    在一般现实时中,第三人称单数后面加上动词的话,动词也要变成单数形式.
    1. 一般动词直接加-s.
    2.  以s,x,z,ch,sh,结尾的单词加-es变化.
    push->pushes
    pass->passes
    catch->catches.
    fix->fixes
    buzz->buzzes
    wash->washes
    3.辅音字母加y结尾,要变y为i加es.
    try->tries.
    worry->worries.
    study-studies.
    cry->cries.
    4.辅音字母o+es
    do->does.
    go->goes.
    在一般现在句变为疑问句，主语是第三人称单数时，原来的主语后面的动词就变为原形，让Does提前.
    Jim plays poker on Sunday.
    Does Jim play poker on Sunday?
    Yes,he does.No,he does not.

    The cat runs along the wall.
    Does the cat run along the wall?
    Yes,it does./No,it does not.

    Donny studies English everyday.
    Does Donny study English everyday?
    Yes,he does./No,he does.

    Example:
    1.那只鸟飞过了村庄
    The bird flies over the village.
    Does the bird fly over the village?
    Yes,it does.No./it doesn't.

    2.Aleen教英文
    Aleen teaches English.
    Does Aleen teach English?
    Yes,he does./No,he doesn't.

    3.妈妈整理了床
     Mother makes the bed.
    Does Mother make the bed?
    Yes,she does./No,she doesn't

    4.她很喜欢苹果
    She likes apples very much.
    Does she like apple very much?
    Yes,she does./No,she doesn't.

    动词的不定式:
    动词的不定式不能做谓语，动词的不定式就是to+动词原型.

    To tell you the truth.告诉你实话吧.(动词不定式短语).

    说是一回事，做又是一回事.
    To say is one thing .To do is another.(动词不定式短语).


######课文录音
    Do you want any meat today,Mrs.Bird?
    Yes,please.
    Do you want beef or lamb?
    Beef,please.
    This lamb's very good.
    I like lamb,but my husband doesn't.
    What about some steak?what about 在这里表示询问的意思，要不.要不一些牛排吧？
    This is a nice piece.
    Give me that piece,please.
    And a pound of mince,too.
    Do you want a chicken,Mrs.Bird?
    They're very nice.
    No,thank you.
    My husband likes steak,
    在主语是第三人称单数引起的陈述句时，肯定句中动词要变单数，
    否定句中在动词前面加doesn't 动词保持原形.
    but he doesn't like chicken.
    To tell you the truth,Mrs.Bird,
    I don't like chicken either!


###### 歌曲欣赏
        Kelly Rowland
        Commandder

    look the forty picture.
    Do you like potatoes?
    Yes,I do.I like potatoes.but I don't one,Tally.

    look the fifty pciture.
    Does Tom  like  cabbages?
    Yes,she does.she likes cabbages.but she doesn't one,Tally.

    look  the sixty picture.
    Does Tom like lettuces?
    Yes,he does.but he doesn't one.

    look the seventy picture.
    Do you like peas?
    Yes,I do,I like peas,but I don't one,Tally.

    look the eighty picture.
    Does Allen like beans?
    Yes,she does,but she doesn't one,Tally.

    look the ninty picture.
    Do you like bananas?
    Yes,I do.I like bananas.but I don't want one,Tally.

    look the twenty picture.
    Mr.Jones likes oranges?
    Yes,he does.he likes oranges.
    but he doesn't one,Tally.

    look the twenty-first picture.
    Does Georage likes apples?
    Yes,he does,he likes apples.
    But he doesn't one,Tally.

    look the twenty-second picture.
    Does Tom  likes pears?
    Yes,he does.he likes pears.
    But he doesn't one,Tally.

    look the twenty-third picture.
    Do you like grapes?
    Yes,I do.I like grapes.
    But I don't one,Tally.

    look the twenty-forth pciture.
    Does Tom likes peaches?
    Yes,he does.he likes peaches.
    But he doesn't one,Tally.
    文章解析
    I like ...
    But he doesn't like..

    choice tomatoes.
    I like choice comatoes.
    But he doesn't like choice tomatoes.

     new potatoes.
     I like new potatoes.
     But he doesn't like new potatoes.

     fresh cabbages
     I like fresh cabbges.
     But he doesn't like fresh cabbages.

     fresh lettuces
     I like fresh lettuces.
     But he doesn't like lettuces.

     garden peas.
     I like garden peas
     But he doesn't like garden peas.

     garden beans
     I like garden beans.
     But he doesn't like garden beans.

     ripe bananas.
     I lke ripe bananas.
     But he doesn't like ripe bananas.

     sweet oranges
     I lke sweet oranges.
     But he doesn't sweet oranges.

     choice apples.
     I like choice apples.
     But he doesn't like choice apples.

     choice pears.
     I like choice pears.
     But he doesn't like choice pears.

     choice grapes.
     I like choice grapes.
     But he doesn't like grapes.

     choice peaches.
     I like choice peaches.
     But he doesn't choice peaches.


######语法精讲
    序数词
    first second third fourth fifth sixth seventh eighth
    ninth tenth elevnth twelfth

    thirteenth 第十三
    fourteenth 第十四
    fifteenth   第十五
    sixteenth   第十六
    seventeenth 第十七
    eigthteenth 第十八
    nineteenth 第十九
    twentieth   第二十
     twenty-first  第二十一
     twenty-second 第二十二
     twenty-third   第二十三
     twenty-fifth 第二十五
     twenty-sixth 第二十六
     twenty-seventh 第二十七
     twenty-eighth 第二十八
     twenty-ninth 第二十九
     thirtieth 第三十
     thirty-fist 第三十一
     thirty-second 第三十二
     thirty-third 第三十三
     以后都是一样的规律

###### 书面练习
     A Complete these sentences using am not,aren't ,isn't,can't,don't,or desn't.

     First. He likes coffe,but I _don't_.
     Second.She liks tea,but he _doesn't_.
     Third.He is eating some bread,but she isn't.(but she isn't eating any bread.)
     fourth. She can type very well,but he can't.(but he can't type very well)
     Fifth. They are working hard,but we aren't(but we aren't working hard)
     sixth. He is reading a magazine.but I am not.(but I am not reading a magazine)

     B Answer these questions using I ,he or she.
     Example:
     Does Penny like tomatoes？
     Yes,she does.
     She likes tomatoes.but she doesn't want any one.

     Do you like potatoes?
     Yes,I'm.
     I like potatoes.but I am not want one.

     First.Does Sam like cabbage?
     Yes,Sam does.
     He likes cabbage.but he doesn't want any.

     Second.Does Sam like lettuce?
     Yes,He does.
     but he does't want any.

     Third.Do you like peas?
     Yes,I do.
     I like peas.but I don't want any.

     Fourth. Does Mrs.White like beans?
       Yes,she does.
       She likes beans,but she doesn't want any.

     Fifth.Do you like bananas?
     Yes,I do.
     I like banans.
     but I don't want any.

     Sixth.Does Mr.Jones like oranges?
     Yes,He does.
     He likes oranges.
     but he don't want any.

     Seventh.Does Geprge like apples?
     Yes,he does.
     He likes apples.
     But he doesn't want any.

     Eighth.Does Elizabeth like pears?
     Yes,She does.
     She likes pears.
     But sha does't want any.

     Ninth.Do you like grapes?
     Yes,I do.
     I like grapes.
     But I don't want one.

     Tenth. Does Carol like peaches?
     Yes,she does.
     She likes peaches.
     but she doesn't want any.

######书面 练习

     主语   第一.第二人称   第三人称
     助动词  Do
     回答   Yes,I/you do.  Yes,he/she/it does.
            No,I/You don't. No,he/she/it does not.

### 51\. <a id="one-fifty-one">lesson fifty-one A pleasant climate<a/>


######单词精讲

>pleasant

    英 ['plez(ə)nt]  美 ['plɛznt]
    adj. 令人愉快的，舒适的；讨人喜欢的，和蔼可亲的
    n. (Pleasant)人名；(英)普莱曾特
    This study is pleasant to work in.
    在这个书房工作是舒适的.
    Andrew seemed very pleasant on the phone.
    安娇在电话里看起来非常和蔼可亲的。


>climate

    英 [ˈklaɪmɪt]  美 [ˈklaɪmɪt]
    n. 气候；风气；思潮；风土

>weather

    英 ['weðə]  美 ['wɛðɚ]
    n. 天气；气象；气候；处境
    vt. 经受住；使风化；侵蚀；使受风吹雨打
    vi. 风化；受侵蚀；经受风雨
    adj. 露天的；迎风的
    n. (Weather)人名；(英)韦瑟

    weather  指短期的天气
    climate 指长期的气候
    What's the weather like ?这个天气怎么样？
    What's the climate like ?这个气候这么怎么样？

>Greece

    英  美 [ɡriːs]
    希腊（欧洲南部国家）

>greek

     [grik]
     n. 希腊人；希腊语
     adj. 希腊的；希腊人的，希腊语的


>spring

    英 [sprɪŋ]  美 [sprɪŋ]
    n. 春天；弹簧；泉水,喷泉；活力；跳跃
    adj. 春天的
    vi. 生长；涌出；跃出；裂开
    vt. 使跳起；使爆炸；突然提出；使弹开
    n. (Spring)人名；(德)施普林；(英、芬、瑞典)斯普林
    [ 过去式 sprang或sprung 过去分词 sprung 现在分词 springing ]

>summer

    英 ['sʌmə]  美 ['sʌmɚ]
    n. 夏季；全盛时期
    vi. 避暑；过夏天
    adj. 夏季的
    n. (Summer)人名；(德)祖默；(英)萨默

>autumn

     英 ['ɔːtəm]  美 ['ɔtəm]
     n. 秋天；成熟期；渐衰期，凋落期
     adj. 秋天的，秋季的
     n. (Autumn)人名；(英)奥特姆

>winter

    英 ['wɪntə]  美 ['wɪntɚ]
    n. 冬季；年岁；萧条期
    vi. 过冬
    adj. 冬天的；越冬的
    n. (Winter)人名；(英、德、匈、罗、捷、西、芬、瑞典、法)温特

>windy

    英 ['wɪndɪ]  美 ['wɪndi]
    adj. 多风的，有风的；腹胀的；吹牛的
    [ 比较级 windier 最高级 windiest ]

>warm

    英 [wɔːm]  美 [wɔrm]
    adj. 温暖的；热情的
    vi. 同情；激动；变温暖
    vt. 使…兴奋；使…温暖；使…感兴趣
    n. 取暖；加热
    n. (Warm)人名；(英)沃姆；(德)瓦姆

>rain

    英 [reɪn]  美 [ren]
    n. 雨；下雨；雨天；雨季
    vi. 下雨；降雨
    vt. 大量地给；使大量落下
    n. (Rain)人名；(法)兰；(英)雷恩；(罗、捷)赖恩
    加后缀y就为adj表示下雨的

>snow

    英 [snəʊ]  美 [sno]
    n. 雪，积雪；下雪
    vi. 降雪
    vt. 使纷纷落下；使变白
    n. (Snow)人名；(英)斯诺
    加后缀y就为adj表示下雪的

月份的说法

    January
    英 ['dʒænjʊ(ə)rɪ]  美 ['dʒænjʊ'ɛri]
    n. 一月

    February
    英 [ˈfebrʊərɪ]  美 [ˈfebrʊerɪ;'fɛbrʊɛrɪ]
    n. 二月

    March
    英 [mɑːtʃ]  美 [mɑrtʃ]
    n. 三月

    April
    英 ['eɪprəl]  美 ['eprəl]
    n. 四月

    May
    英 [meɪ]  美 [me]
    n. 五月

    June
    英 [dʒu:n]  美 [dʒun]
    n. 六月；琼（女名）

    July
    英 [dʒʊˈlaɪ]  美 [dʒʊˈlaɪ]
    n. 七月

    august
    英 [ɔ:ˈgʌst]  美 [ɔˈɡʌst]
    adj. 威严的；令人敬畏的
    n. 八月（简写为Aug）
    n. (August)人名；(法、葡、西、俄、罗、英、德、瑞典、挪)奥古斯特

    September
    英 [sep'tembə]  美 [sɛp'tɛmbɚ]
    n. 九月

    October
    英 [ɒk'təʊbə]  美 [ɑk'tobɚ]
    n. [天] 十月

    November
    英 [nə(ʊ)'vembə]  美 [no'vɛmbɚ]
    n. 十一月

    December
    英 [dɪ'sembə]  美 [dɪ'sɛmbɚ]
    n. 十二月


###### 课文录音

     HANS:Where do you come from?
     DIMITRI: I come from Greeece.
     HANS:What's the climate like in your country?
     DIMITRI:It's very pleasant.
     HANS:What's the weather like in spring?
     DIMITRI:It's often  windy in March.
             It's always warm in April and May.
             But it rains sometimes.
     HANS: What's it like in summer?
     DIMITRI:It's always hot in June,July and August.
             The sun shines every day.
      HANS:Is it cold or warm in autumn?
      DIMITRI:It's always warm in September and October.
              It's often cold in November  and it rains sometimes.
      HANS:  Is it very cold in winter?
      DIMITRI:It's often cold in December,January,and February.
      It snows sometimes.
        文章解析
        Where do you come from?
        I come from China.

        Where are you from?
        I am from China.

        I come from Greece.
        What's the climate like in your country?
        What +be动词+like?
        What...like?这一句型一般用于询问事物的状况.
        如天气，气候，或询问任务或事物的外观或特征.
        What's the weather like today?今天的天气这么样？
        What is your house like?你的房子怎么样？
        What is his suit like?你的西装怎么样？
        What is the weather like tomorrow?明天的天气这么样？

        频率副词
        often
        英 ['ɒf(tə)n]  美 [ˈɔ:fn; ɔfən]
        adv. 常常，时常
        [ 比较级 more often 或 oftener 最高级 most often 或 oftenest ]

        sometimes 有时
         英 ['sʌmtaɪmz]  美 ['sʌmtaɪmz]
         adv. 有时，间或

        always 总是
        英 [ˈɔ:lweɪz]  美 ['ɔlwez]
        adv. 永远，一直；总是；常常

        usually 通常
        英 [ˈjuːʒʊəlɪ]  美 [juʒəlɪ]
        adv. 通常，经常

        never 从未
        英 ['nevə]  美 ['nɛvɚ]
        adv. 从未；决不

        频率副词一般放在be动词之后，行为动词之前.
        She is often late她经常迟到。
        I am often  go swim.去经常去游泳。
        Jam always goes to the supermarket.吉姆总是去超市.
        Jason never smokes.杰森从来不抽烟
        Ilian usually tells me his stroy.伊莲通常告诉我她的故事.

       It's always warm in April and May,
       but it rains sometimes.这句话中的sometimes没有放在行为动词之前，是一个例外。
       sometimes是可以放在句末的，表示有时。
       but it sometimes rains。和but it rains sometimes.意思是一样的.


######口语快门
    如何去恭喜别人

     用congratulations
     congratulations
     美 [kən,grætʃə'leʃənz]
     n. 祝贺；恭喜；贺词（congratulation的复数形式）

    driving license:驾照
    driving test:驾照考试

    A:I passed my driving test.我通过了驾考考试.
    congratulations. 恭喜.

    congratulations on sth.恭喜你在某事上.

    engaged
    英 [ɪn'geɪdʒd; en-]  美 [ɪn'gedʒd]
    adj. 使用中的，忙碌的
    v. 保证；约定；同…订婚（engage的过去分词）
    engagement
    英 [ɪn'geɪdʒm(ə)nt; en-]  美 [ɪn'ɡedʒmənt]
    n. 婚约；约会；交战；诺言
    n. 参与度（指用户点赞、转发、评论、下载文档、观看视频、咨询等交互行为）

    A.I am engaged.我订婚了.
    B.Congratulations.恭喜.
    Congratulations on your engagement.恭喜你订婚了。

    Congratulations on your marriage!恭喜你结婚。
    Congratulations on entering Nanjing University!恭喜进入南京大学。

     promotion
     英 [prə'məʊʃn]  美 [prə'moʃən]
     n. 提升，[劳经] 晋升；推销，促销；促进；发扬，振兴
    Congratulations on your promotion!恭喜你升职了.

    recovery
    英 [rɪ'kʌv(ə)rɪ]  美 [rɪ'kʌvəri]
    n. 恢复，复原；痊愈；重获
    [ 复数 recoveries ]
    Congratulations on your complete recovery.恭喜你康复了.

    way to go.(短语)也可以表示祝贺的意思.上面所有的情况都可以用way to go 表示.


###### 歌曲欣赏

        Shakira
        She Wolf

### 52\. <a id="one-fifty-two">fifty-two What are they nationnality?Where do they come form?<a/>

######单词精讲

>Brazil

    英 [brə'zil]  美
    n. 巴西（拉丁美洲国家）

>Brazilian

    英 [brəˈzɪliən]  美 [brə'zɪljən]
    adj. 巴西的；巴西人的
    n. 巴西人

>Holland

    英 ['hɒlənd]  美 ['hɑlənd]
    n. 荷兰

>Dutch

    英 [dʌtʃ]  美 [dʌtʃ]
    adj. 荷兰的；荷兰人的；荷兰语的
    n. 荷兰人；荷兰语
    adv. 费用平摊地；各自付账地

###### 听录音
    Look the twentieth picture.
    Do you come from brazil?
    No,I don't come from brazil.
    I come from the U.S。

    Look the twenty-first picture.
    Does she come from the U.S.
    No,she doesn't come from the U.S.
    She comes from the brazile.

    Look the  twenty-second picture.
    Does she come from England?
    No,she doesn't come from England.
    She comes from holland.

    Look the twenty-third picture.
    Do you both come from holland?
    No,we don't come from holland.
    We come from England.

    Look the twenty-forth picture.
    Do they come from Germany?
    No,they don't come from Germany.
    They come from France.

    Look the twenty-fifth picture.
    Do I come from France?
    No,you don't form France.
    You come from Germany.

    Look the twenty-sixth picture.
    Does he come from  Italy.
    No,he doesn't come from Italy.
    He come from Greece.

    you come from Italy.


###### 书面练习

    A Complete these sentences.

    Example:
    I come from England.
    But Stella comes form Spain.

    one.We come from Germany,
    But Dimitri _comes_ from Greece.

    two.I like cold weather.
    But he _likes_ warm weather.

    three.He comes from the U.S .
    but She _comes_ from Endland.

    four.She doesn't like the winter.
    But she _likes_ the summer.

    five.I come from Norway,
    but you _come_ from Spain.

    six.Stella comes from Spain,
    But Hans and Karl _come_ from Germany.
    这里的come做原形,Hans和Karl一起表示人称的复数，就不是第三人称单数了,所以用原形。
    seven.We don't come from Spain.
    We come form Brazil.

    B.Write questions and answers.
    Example:
    he/(Brazil)/the U.S
    Where does he come from?
    Does he come from Brazil?
    No,he doesn't come from Brazil.
    He comes from the U.S.
    What nationality is he?
    He's American.

    one.She/(England)/the U.S
    Where does she come from?
    Does she come from England?
    No,she doesn't come from England.
    She comes from the U.S.
    What nationality is she?
    She is American.

    two. they/(France)/England
    Where do they come from?
    Do they come from France?
    No,they don't come from France.
    They come from England.
    What nationality are they?
    They are English.

    three.he/(France)/Germany
    Where does he come from?
    Does he come from France?
    No,he doesn't come from France.
    He comes form Germany.
    What nationality is he?
    He is Germen.

    four.he/(Italy)/Greece
    Where does he come from?
    Does he come from Italy?
    No,he doesn't come from Italy.
    He comes from Greece（希腊）.
    What nationality is he ?
    He is Greek(希腊人).

    five.they/(Greece)/Italy
    Where do they come from?
    Do they come from Greece?
    No,they don't come from Greece.
    They come from Italy.
    What nationality are they?
    They are Italian.

    six.they/(Brazil)/Norway
    Where do they come from?
    Do the y come from Brazil?
    No,they don't come from Brazil.
    They come from Norway.
    What nationality are they?
    They are norwegians.

    seven.they/(Norway)Greece.
    Where do they come from?
    Do they come form Norway?
    No,they don't come from Norway.
    They come from Greece.
    What nationality are they?
    They are Greek.

    eight.she/(Italy)/Spain
    Where does she come from?
    Does she come from Italy?
    No,she doesn't come from Italy.
    She comes from Spain.
    What nationality is she?
    She is Spanish.

    nine.she/(Norway)/France
    Where does she  come from?
    Does she come form Norway?
    No,she doesn't come from Norway.
    She comes from France.
    What nationality is she?
    She is French.

    ten. he /(the U.S)/Brazil
    Where does he come from?
    Does he come from the U.S?
    No,he doesn't come from the U.S。
    He comes from Brazil(巴西).
    What nationality is he?
    He is Brazilian（巴西人）.

     重点回顾.
     Where does he/she come from?他/她来自哪里.(问的是来自哪个国家)
     Where do you/they come from?

     Does she/he/Stella come from....?
     Do you/we/they come from...?

     Yes,he/she does./No,she/he doesn't.
     Yes,you/they/I do./No,you/they/I don't.

    What nationality is he?他是哪个国籍？(表示问他是哪国人?)

        M2M
      The Day You Went Away

### 53\. <a id="one-fifty-three">lesson fifty-three An interesting climate<a/>


######单词精讲

>mild

    mild
    英 [maɪld]  美 [maɪld]
    adj. 温和的；轻微的；淡味的；文雅的；不含有害物质的的
    n. （英国的一种）淡味麦芽啤酒
    n. (Mild)人名；(瑞典)米尔德；(德、捷、芬)米尔德
    1.(天气等)温暖的，温和的
    They have a mild winter this year.
    他们今年有一个温暖的冬天.
    2.(形容的一个认的性格等)温和的
    John is a mild man.焦恩是一个温和的人.
    3(食物等)味淡的
    This dish is very mild.
    这道菜是非常味淡的.
    The winter here is always mild.

>north

    英 [nɔːθ]  美 [nɔrθ]
    n. 北，北方
    adj. 北方的；朝北的
    adv. 在北方，向北方
    Harbin is i n the north of china.
>east

    英 [iːst]  美 [ist]
    n. 东方；东风；东方国家
    adj. 东方的；向东的；从东方来的
    adv. 向东方，在东方
    n. (East)人名；(英)伊斯特


>west

    英 [west]  美 [wɛst]
    n. 西；西方；西部
    adj. 西方的；朝西的
    adv. 在西方；向西方；自西方
    n. (West)人名；(英、德、芬、瑞典)韦斯特


>south

    英 [saʊθ]  美 [saʊθ]
    n. 南方，南边；南部
    adv. 在南方，向南方
    adj. 南的，南方的
    n. (South)人名；(老)苏；(英)索思
    Shanghai is a south city in china.


>wet

    英 [wet]  美 [wɛt]

    [ 比较级 wetter 最高级 wettest 过去式 wet 或 wetted 过去分词 wet 或 wetted 现在分词 wetting ]
    The weather is very wet.
>dry

    英 [draɪ]  美 [draɪ]

>season

>best

    英 [best]  美 [bɛst]
    n. 最好的人，最好的事物；最佳状态
    adj. 最好的
    adv. 最好地
    vt. 打败，胜过
    n. (Best)人名；(英、西、德、葡、法)贝斯特
    best 放在句末，表示最喜欢地.最著名样.
    I like football best.我最喜欢足球。
    I like hot pot best。我最喜欢火锅
    可以表示最好的,最棒的.
    You are the best表示你是最棒/好的。
    Brazil is the best team.巴西是最棒的球队。

>night

    英 [naɪt]  美 [naɪt]

    vi. 上升；增强；起立；高耸
    vt. 使…飞起；使…浮上水面
    n. 上升；高地；增加；出现
    [ 过去式 rose 过去分词 risen 现在分词 rising ]
    1(日，月等)升起
    The sun is rising。太阳正在升起
    2（河水,物价，温度等）上涨.
    The price of pork is still rising.
    猪肉的价格持续上升.
    3.起床，起身,
    Rise and shine. 谚语(起床天阳出来了)

    英 [ˈsʌbdʒɪkt;(for adj.)ˈsʌbdʒɪkt;(for v.)səbˈdʒekt] 美 [ˈsʌbdʒɪkt;(for adj.)ˈsʌbdʒɪkt;(for v.)səbˈdʒɛkt]

    adj. 服从的；易患…的；受制于…的
    vt. 使…隶属；使屈从于…

>conversation

    英 [kɒnvə'seɪʃ(ə)n]  美 [,kɑnvɚ'seʃən]
    n. 交谈，会话；社交；交往，交际；会谈；（人与计算机的）人机对话

######课文录音

    Listen fifty-three and An interesing climate.
    listen to the table,and answers the questions.

    HANS:Where do you come from？
    JIM:I come from  England.
    HANS:What's the climate like in your country?
    JIM:It's mild,but it's not always pleasant.
    JIM:The weather's often cold in the North and windy in the East.
        It's often wet in the West and sometimes warm in the South.
    HANS:Which seasons do you like best?
    JIM:I like spring and summer.The days are long and the nights are short.
        The sun rises early and sets late.
    JIM:I don't like autumn and winter.
        he days are short and the nights are long.The sun rises late and sets early.
    JIM:Our cimate is not very good,but it's certainly interesting.
        It's our favourite subject of conversation.

    文章解析
    The weather's often cold in the North and windy in the East
    表示一个国家或地区的方位词如果单独使用，方位词首字母一般需要大写。
    而仅仅表示方位意义的方位词则不需要大写。
    the north wind.这个北边的风.
    south window 南方的窗户.
    本课小结
    north,east,west,south
    What is the climate like in your coutry?
    What is the weather like in your coutry?
    Which seasons do you like best?
    I like spring and summer best.
    my favourite climate is spring and summer.

###### 歌曲欣赏
    Sarah Connor
    Just One Last Dance

     Where does she come from?
     Is she Turkish?
     Yes,she comes from Turkey.

     文章解析:
     What nationality are they?
     Where do they come from?


###### 书面练习
    A. Write questins and answers.
    Example:
    The sun rises early.
    Does the sun rise early?
    The sun doesn't rise early.

    one.The sun sets late.
        Does the sun set late?
        The sun doesn't set late.

     two.He likes ice cream.
        Does he like ice cream?
        He doesn't like ice cream.

     three.Mrs.Jones wants a biscuit.
          Does  Mrs.Jones  want a biscuit?
          Mr.s Jones doesn't want a biscuit.

     Four. Jim comes from England.
           Does Jim come from England?
          Jim doesn't come from England.


    B.Write questions and answers using these words.
    模仿例句并回答
     Example:
     he/Brazil
     Where does he come from?Is he Brazilian?
     Yes,He's Brazilian.He comes from Brazil.

     One.he/Australia
     Where does he come from?Is he Australian?
     Yes,He is Australian.He comes from Austranlia.

     Two.he/Austria
      Where does he come from?Is he Austrian?
      Yes,he's Austrian.he comes from Austria.

      Three.He/Canada
      Where does he come from?Is he Canadian?
      Yes,he is Canadian.He comes from Canada.

      Four.They/china
      Where do they come from?Are they chinese?
      Yes.They are chinese.They come from china.

      Five.he/Finland
      Where does he come from？Is he finnish?
      Yes,He is Finnish.He comes from Finlan.

      Six.She/India.
      Where does she come from?Is she indian?
      Yes,she is indian.She comes from india.

      Seven.they/Japan
      Where do they come from?Are they Japanese?
      Yes,they are Japanese.They come from Japan.

      Eight.they/Nigeria
      Where do they come from?Are they Nigerian?
      Yes,they are nigerian.They come from Nigeria.

      Nine.she/Turkey
      Where does she come from?Is she Turkish?
      Yes,she is Turkish.She comes from Turkey.

      Ten.she/Korea
      Where does she come from?Is she korean?
      Yes,she is korean.She comes from korea.

 ######口语快门
      与天气相关

      How is the weather?天气如何？(这个句子后面，可以加时间，表示这个时间天气如何)
      How is the weather tomorrow?明天天气如何?
      How is the weather next week?下周天气如何?
      What is the weather like?天气如何?

      询问气温

      What is the temperature today?今天气温多少？
      The temperature today is 40 degree(度).今天温度是40度.

      weather forecast.天气预报.
      What does the weather forecast say?天气预报怎么说？

      询问家乡的气候。
      What is the climate like in your country/hometown(家乡)?

      gloomy
      英 ['gluːmɪ]  美 ['ɡlumi]
      adj. 黑暗的；沮丧的；阴郁的
      [ 比较级 gloomier 最高级 gloomiest ]


      如何说一个天气
      It is a lovely day.今天是可爱好的天。
      It is very cloudy.
      It is very gloomy.今天是阴霾的。
      It is very hot today.
      It is very cold today.
      It is freezing today.今天正在结冰了.
      It is very windy today.

        breezy
        英 ['briːzɪ]  美 ['brizi]
        adj. 有微风的；轻松愉快的；通风好的；活泼的
        [ 比较级 breezier 最高级 breeziest ]

      It's nice and breezy here. 今天是晴朗和有微风的在这里。

      It's raining cats and dogs outside(在外面).(美语中的俚语)在外面正在下倾盆大雨/暴雨.

      clear up.放晴。
      It is clearing up.天气正在放晴.

### 55\. <a id="one-fifty-five">lesson  fifty-five The Sawyer family<a/>

###### 单词精讲

>live

    英 [laɪv；lɪv]  美 [laɪv；lɪv]
    adj. 活的；生动的；实况转播的；精力充沛的
    vt. 经历；度过
    vi. 活；居住；生存
    n. (Live)人名；(法)利夫
    1.v.居住，生活 （读 lɪv）
    I live in Nanjing.

    2.活，生存.
    Fish can't live long out of water.
    鱼长时间离开水就不能生活了。

    3.v.靠...生活(by/on)
    He lives by playing the violin.他靠小提琴生活.

    4.adj. 现场的.直播的 .(做形容词此时读 laɪv)

    live +介词 动词短语

    live in :住在一个比较大的地方（国家，城市）
    He lives in America.

    live at:住在一个比较小的地方（区，街道）
    I live at Wangzi Street。我住在王子街.

>stay

    英 [steɪ]  美 [ste]
    vi. 停留；坚持；暂住；停下
    vt. 坚持；暂住；抑制
    n. 逗留；停止；支柱
    [ 过去式 stayed 或 staid 过去分词 stayed 或 staid 现在分词 staying ]

    stay here.待在这边.
    He likes to stay at home.他喜欢待在家里.

>home

      英 [h����m]  美 [hom]
      n. 家，住宅；产地；家乡；避难所

      [ 过去式 homed 过去分词 homed 现在分词 homing ]
    home ：指家庭的住址所再
    family: 指家庭远程总称.

    I get home 我到家了.
    homework 家庭作业
    英 ['həʊmwɜːk]  美 ['hom'wɝk]

    homeless(此时less表示后缀的作用,表示否定的意思)无家可归的人.

>together

    英 [t��'ge����]  美 [t��'��������]

    adj. 新潮的；情绪稳定的，做事有效率的

     We are together 我们在一起.

>arrive

    英 [ə'raɪv]  美 [ə'raɪv]
    vi. 到达；成功；达成；出生
    n. (Arrive)人名；(法)阿里夫
    arrive in... 到达某地...
    The train arrives in London at 8:20 p.m.
    2来临
    At last（最终）,the day of graduation arrives.最终，毕业这一天来临了.

    arrive in:到达(大地方)
    The plane arrives in New York.

    arrive at;到达(小地方)
    The train arrives at the King Street。这个火车到达国王街.


###### 课文录音

    The Sawyers live at 87 King Street.
    Sawyers 索叶(人名)
    The(定冠词) +名字+s:表示一家人.(定冠词the加名词的加s形式，表示这个名字的人的一家人.)

    In the morning,Mr.Sawyer goes to work and the children go to school.
    go to work  上班 go to shcool上学

    Their father takes them to school every day.
    take....to.... 带...去...
    Mrs.Sawyer stays at home every day.

    She does the housework.

    She always eats her lunch at noon.
    In the afternoon,she usually sees her friends.
    They often drink tea together.
    In the evening,the children come home from school.
    come home（固定短语）回家.

    They arrive home early.
    arrive home(固定搭配,arrive 与hom连用时不要后面不要加介词)表示到家
    Mr.Sawyer comes home from work.
    He arrives home late.
    At night,the children always do their homework.
    Then they go to bed.
    Mr.Sawyer usually reads his newspaper,but sometimes he and his wife watch television.

      look the thirty-fouth picture.
      What does he often do in the evening?
      He often reads his newspaper in the evening.


######书面练习

    A Complete these sentences using -s or -es.
     Exaple:
     She washes the dishes every day.

     one. The children go to school in the morning.

     two. Their father takes them to school.

     three.Mrs.Sawyer stays at home.

     four. She does the housework.

     five.She always eats her lunch at noon.

     B.Write questions and answers.
     Example:
     she/moring    often/dust/the cupboard.
     What does she do in the moring?
     She often dusts the cupboard in the morning.

     1. she/morning always/make/the bed.
       What does she do in the morning？
       She always makes the bed in the morning.

     2.he/moring  always/shave
     What deos he do in the morning?
     He always shaves in the moring.

     3.they/evening sometimes/listen to/the stereo
      What do they do in the evening?
      They sometimes listen to the stereo in the evening.

      4.he/every day  always/clean /the blackboard
      What does he do every day?
      He always cleans the blackboard every day.

      5.they/night always /go /to bed early
      What do they do at night?
      They  always go to bed  early at night.

      6.she/every day  usually /wash/the dishes
      What does she do every day?
      She usually washes the dishes every day.

      7.they /afternoon  usually /type /some letters
      What do they do afternoon?
      They  usually type  some letters in the afternoon.

       8.it/ every day usually/drink some milk
       What does it do every day?
       It  usually drinks some milk every day.

       9.they/evening sometimes/watch /television.
       What do they do in the eventing?
       They sometimes watch television in the evening.

       10.she/noon always /eat/ her lunch
       What does she do at noon?
       She always eats her lunch at noon.

       11.he/evening  often/read/his newspaper
       What does he do in the evening?
       He often reads his newspaper in the evening.

######口语快门

        说友谊
        Forget me not.(短语)勿忘我。
        Stay in touch .(短语)保持联络
        Don't be a stranger.不要成为一个陌生人
        You are like a borther/sister to me.

        A friend in need is a friend indeed.一个朋友在需要的时候是一个真正的朋友.

### 57\. <a id="one-fifty-seven">lesson An unusual day<a/>


######单词精讲

>o'clock

     英 [ə'klɒk]  美 [ə'klɑk]
     abbr. …点钟（等于of the clock）
     a.m. 上午
     p.m. 下午

>moment

    英 ['məʊm(ə)nt]  美 ['momənt]
    n. 片刻，瞬间，时刻；重要，契机
    n. (Moment)人名；(英)莫门特

    问时间。
    What is the time?
    What time is it?
    It's nine o'olock a.m.上午9点钟。
    It's four o'clock p.m.下午4点钟
    1说整点钟：
    three o'clock 三点钟    five o'clock 五点钟  twelve o'clock
    2.几点过几分
    （1）在点钟后的1-30分钟之内
    It's 分钟 psat 点钟.
    It's eight past three.3点零把分钟.(它是八分钟过了3点钟，就表示几点钟几分)
    =Tt's three eight.

    It's twenty past five.=It's five twenty. 3点20分.

    （2）半点之后:It's 分钟 to 点钟.
     （某个钟点的31分到下一个整点的时候，在过半点之后常用介词to）
     It's twenty to seven.(表示离7点还有20分钟) 就表示6点4分钟.
     =It's six forty.
     It's twenty-five to twelve.11点35分.
     =It's eleven thirty-five.

    (3)半点：It's half past 点钟.
    It's half past ten.10点半了。 It's half past three.3三点半了.

    (5)一刻钟：quarter
    It's a quarter past three.3点15分。
    It's quarter to two.1点15分。
    （quater 不可以It's +点钟+ quarter 这样的句型）
    (6)at ：表示在什么时间点
    I go to bed at ten to twelve.我睡觉在11点50分.
    She  arrive here at twenty to four.她在3点40达到这里.

    It's five twenty= It'stwenty past five 5:20
    It's four ten = It's ten past four 4:10
    It's twelve fouty-fvie=It's fivteen/quarter to thirteen/one 12:45
    It's eighteen fivteen=It's fivteen/quarter past eighteen 18:15
    It's ten thirty-five = It's twenty-five to eleven 10:35
    It's half past nine =It's nine thirty.9:30
    It's thirteen twenty-four=It's  twenty-four past thirteen. 13:24

###### 课文录音

      It's eigth o'clock.
      The children go to shcoll by car every day,
      but today,they are going to school on foot.
      It is ten o'clock.
      Mrs.Sawyer usually stays at home in the morning,
      But this morning,she is going to the shops.
      It's four o'clock.
      In the afternoon.Mrs.Sawyer usually drinks tea in the living room.
      But this afternoon,she is drinking tea in the garden.
      It's six o'clock.
      In the evening,the children usually do their homework,
      but this evening,they are not doing their homework.
      At the moment(在此刻),they are playing in the garden.
      It's nine o'clock.
      Mr.Sawyer usually reads his newspaper at night.
      But he's not reading his newspaper tonight.
      At the moment,he's reading an interesting book.

      一般现在时：表示某个习惯性动作。
     通常一般现在常有usually ,always,often,sometimes,never.的句式表示
     一般现在时.

     现在进行时：表示此时此刻正在进行的动作
     现在进行时中，是某个时刻正在进行的动作，而不是反复重复性的动作。
     现在进行时的时间通常是now,at the moment,today.this afternoon.this evening,tonight.

 ###### 口语快门

    Sleep tight.美美睡上一觉
    Good night and sleep tight. 晚安美美睡上一觉
    rise and shine.天阳晒屁股了.（就叫别人起床的意思。）

### 58\. <a id="one-fifty-eight">lesson  fifty-eight What's the time<a/>

###### 单词精讲




###### 听录音
        listen fifty-eight
        repetition dirll

       What does he usually do every day?
       He usually  shaves at seven o'colok every day.
       What's he doing today?
       He's shaveing at eight o'clock today.

       What does she usually do in the morning?
       She usualy drinks tea in the morning.
       What's she doing this morning?
       She is drinking coffee in the morning.

       What do they usually do in the afternoon?
       They usually play in the garden in the afternoon.
       What are they doing this afternoon?
       They are swmming in the river this afternoon.

       What do you usually do in the evening?
       I usually cook a meal in the evening.
       What are you doing this evening?
       I'am reading a book this evening.

       What do you usually do at night?
       We usually wacth television at night.
       What are you  doing tonight?
       We are listening to stereo tonight.

###### 书面练习

        A Complete these sentences.
        Example:
        He usually shaves at 7.00 o'clock,but today.
        He is shaving at 8.00.

        frist. She usually drinks tea in the morning,
        but this morning,she is drinking coffee.

        Second.They usually play in the garden in teh afternoon.
        But,this afternoon,they are playing in the park.

        Third.He usually washes the dishes at night.
        But tonight he is washing clothes.

        B Write questions and answers following the pattern in the example.
        Exaples:
        They/every day   go/to schoolk by car
        What do they usually do every day?
        They usually go to school by car every day.

        today go/to school on foot
        What are they doing today?
        They are going to school on foot toady.

        she/morning   drink/tea
        morning       drink/cofee

        What does she  usually do in the mornng？
        she usually drinks tea in the morning.
        What is she doing this mornng?
        She is drinking cofee this morning.

        2.they/ afternoon  play/in the garden
        afternoon   swim/n the river
        What do they usually do in the afternoon?
        They  usually play in the garden in the afternoon.
        What are they doing this afternoon?
        They are swiming in the river this afternoon.

        3.I/ evening cool/a meal
         evening     read/a book
         What do you usually do in the evening?
         I usually cook a meal in the eveing.
         What are you doing this evening?
         I am reading a book this evening.

        4.we/ night  watch /television
          tonigh       listen to/the stereo
          What do you usually do  at night?
          We usualy watch television at night
          What are you doing  tonight?
          We are listening to the stereo tonigh.


######口语快门
        问别人有没有空

        Are you free? 你有空吗?
        Are you free this weekend?这个周末你有空吗？
        I am free this weekend. 我是有空的这个周末.

        Are you doing anything?你正在做任何事吗？
        Are you doing anything this afternoon?这个下午你正在做任何事吗？
        I am not doing anything this afternoon.这个下午我没有做任何事.

        plan
        Do you have plans for this Sunday?这个星期天你有安排吗？
        No,I don't have any plans for this Sunday.不，我没有任何计划这个星期天.

        busy 忙碌

        Are you busy?
        Are you busy this evening?这个晚上你忙吗 ？

        否定回答的时候.
        如何去拒绝自己没有空.
        Sorry,I am tied up.对不起，我被绳子捆起来了 。就表示我脱不开身。
        Sorry,I haves plans.对不起，我有安排了。
        Sorry,I am busy.对不起，我是忙碌的.
        I am afraid I can't.我恐怕我无法赴约.

        加入别人答应了我们的邀请

        Let's =let us 让我们一起

        let's go out for a drink。让我们喝一杯吧。
        Let's go see a movie.让我们去看一场电影
        Let's go swimming /shopping/traveling.让我们去游泳/购物/旅游.
        (此时的go 后的动词要变为现在分词形式，是固定搭配)
        Let's have dinner together.让我们一起吃完饭吧。

        How about +doing someing
        做什么事怎么样？
        Let's go out for a drink.
        How about going out for a drink?
        出去喝饮料怎么样？
       Let's go see a movie.
       How about going see a movie?

       Let's  go swimming/shopping/traveling
       How about going swimming/shopping/traveling?
       去游泳/购物/旅游/怎么样？
       Let's have dinner together.
       How about having dinner together?
       去吃晚饭如何？

        区别
        Let's +do +sth  表示陈述
        How about +doing +sth 表示疑问.

         Wanna Be

### 59\. <a id="one-fifty-nine">lesson  fifty-nine Is that all? <a/>

######单词精讲

>envelope

    英 ['envələʊp; 'ɒn-]
    n. 信封，封皮；包膜；[天] 包层；包迹

>writing paper 信纸

    writing paper 是不可数的
    paper 不可数的   表示数量时要用piece数量词  a piece of paper 一张纸
    可数名词：newspaper  可以变为复数形式

>shop assistant

    售货员

>size

    英 [saɪz]  美 [saɪz]
    n. 大小；尺寸
    adj. 一定尺寸的
    vt. 依大小排列
    vi. 可比拟
    [ 过去式 sized 过去分词 sized 现在分词 sizing ]

>special

    英 ['speʃ(ə)l]  美 [ˈspɛʃəl]
    n. 特使，特派人员；特刊；特色菜；专车；特价商品
    adj. 特别的；专门的，专用的
    [ 比较级 more special 最高级 most special ]

    special size 特定的尺寸
    large size 大的尺寸
    medium size 中间的尺寸
    small siez 小的尺寸
    pocket size  袖珍尺寸
    portable size 便携式尺寸


>pad

    英 [pæd]  美 [pæd]
    n. 衬垫；护具；便笺簿；填补
    vi. 步行；放轻脚步走
    vt. 填补；走
    n. (Pad)人名；(英)帕德(男子教名 Patrick 的昵称)

>glue

    英 [gluː]  美 [ɡlu] 不可数
    vt. 粘合；似胶般固着于
    n. 胶；各种胶合物
    [ 过去式 glued 过去分词 glued 现在分词 gluing ]
     a bottle of glue 一瓶胶水

>chalk

    英 [tʃɔːk]  美 [tʃɔk]  不可数
    vt. 用粉笔写；用白垩粉擦；记录；规划
    n. 粉笔；白垩；用粉笔划的记号
    adj. 用粉笔写的
    vi. 变成白垩状
    n. (Chalk)人名；(英)乔克
    a peice of  chalk 一支粉

>change

    英 [tʃeɪn(d)ʒ]  美 [tʃendʒ]
    vt. 改变；交换
    n. 变化；找回的零钱
    vi. 改变；兑换
    [ 过去式 changed 过去分词 changed 现在分词 changing ]
    1.n.零钱(不可数)
    I have no change with me.我没有带零钱
    2.n.变化，转换(可数)
    Let's go to a French restaurant for a change.
    (for a change  改变一下 固定搭配)
    3.v.改变
    I want to change my life.我想改变我的生活.
    I want to chage a school.我想改变一个学校.

>have:


    英 [həv;hæv]  美 [həv;hæv]
    vt. 有；让；拿；从事；允许
    aux. 已经
    n. (Have)人名；(芬)哈韦；(德)哈弗
    [ 第三人称单数 has 过去式 had 过去分词 had 现在分词 having ]
    肯定陈述句：
    I  have a sister.
    He has a car.
    we have a beautiful  school.
    They have a footbal team.

    have/has的否定形式
    1当have/has 表示’拥有，具有‘时
    (1).have/has+not
    (2) don't/doesn't +have 这种形式用的比较多 (当主语是第三人称单数时,have前加doesn't,have如果是has要变为have)

    I have a sister.
    I don't have a sister.
    He has a car.
    He doesn't have a car.

     2.当have/has 表示行为动词(一个动作)时
     eat/have one's lunch吃午餐
     take/have some medicine 吃一些药
     have a chat/tale 聊天
     take /have a  rest/break  休息一下
     drink/have a cup of coffee 喝一杯咖啡

     当has/have 表示行为动词时(一个具体的动作)时
     不可以在have/has后面加not.要借助助动词do来表示否定和疑问.
     don't/doesn't +have
     I have/eat my lunch at twelve every day.每天中午12点我吃我的午餐？
     否定：I don't have/eat my lunch at twelve every dat.
     Do you have your lunch at twelve every dat?

     He has his midicine at five o'clock every day.他在5点钟吃一些药.
     He doesn't have his midicine at five o'clock every day.他没有在5点钟吃他的药.
     Does he have his midicine at five o'clock every day？他有在每天5点钟吃药吗？

     书面练习  当have表示一个行为动词时变为否定形式和疑问形式.
     1.He always has a break after study.(has a break 休息一下)
      He doesn't always have a break after study.
      Does he always have a break after study？

     2.The dog usually has a bone for dinner.
      The dog doesn't usually have a bone for dinner.
      Does the dog usually have a bone for dinner?

     3.We have coffee in the garden.
      we don't  have coffee in the garden.
      Do we have coffee in the garden?

     4.I have a talk/chat with him about the money.
       I don't have a  talk/chat with him about the money.
       Do I have a talk/chat with him about the money?

###### 课文录音

    listen fifty-nine
    Is that all?
    listen to the table,Then answers the questions.
    Does Aelly buy any chalk?

    I want some envelopes,please.
    我想要一些信封。
    Do you want the large size or the small size？
    你想要大号的信封还是小号的？
    这个句型的疑问句是选择疑问句,回答时不用yes,直接回答要的选择就可以了。
    The large size,please.
    这个大号的 .
    Do you have any writing paper?
    你有任何的信纸吗？
    Yes,we do.
    是的，我们有.
    I don't have any small pads.
    我没有任何的小点信纸
    I only have large ones.Do you want a  pad?
    我仅仅只有大的信纸。你想要一本信纸吗？
    Yes,please.And I want some glue.
    是的，请给我一本。和我想要一些胶水
    A bottle of glue.
    一瓶胶水
    And I want a large box of chalk,too.
    我也想要一大盒粉笔
    I only have small boxes.
    我仅仅只有小盒的.
    Do you want one?
    你要一盒吗？
    No,thank you.
    不，谢谢。
    Lady:No,thank you .
    Is that all？ 就这些吗？
    That's all.thank you.
    就这些，谢谢。
    What else do you want?
     你想要其他的什么吗？
     (What else do you like? 你喜欢其他的什么吗？)
    I want my change.
     我想要我的零钱。(就是你要找我零钱啊).

 ###### 口语快门
    如何谈论校园的专业
     major
     英 ['meɪdʒə]  美 ['medʒɚ]
     adj. 主要的；重要的；主修的；较多的
     n. [人类] 成年人；主修科目；陆军少校
     vi. 主修
     n. (Major)人名；(西)马霍尔；(法)马若尔；(捷、德、塞、瑞典)马约尔；(英)梅杰

     英 [ə'brɔːd]  美 [ə'brɔd]

### 61\. <a id="one-sixty-one">lesson  sixty-one A bad cold（重感冒）<a/>

###### 单词精讲

>feel

    英 [fiːl]  美 [fil]
    vt. 感觉；认为；触摸；试探
    vi. 觉得；摸索
    n. 感觉；触摸
    [ 过去式 felt 过去分词 felt 现在分词 feeling ]
    1觉得，感觉，意识到
    I feel rain on my face.我感觉到雨在我脸上.
    He  is feeling better well today.他今天感觉好一点了.
    2.摸，触：（客体）给认某种感觉
    The silk feels very smooth. 这个丝绸触感非常光滑的.

>smooth

    英 [smuːð]  美 [smʊð]
    adj. 顺利的；光滑的；平稳的
    vt. 使光滑；消除（障碍等）；使优雅；缓和
    n. 平滑部分；一块平地
    vi. 变平静；变平滑
    adv. 光滑地；平稳地；流畅地
    [ 比较级 smoother 最高级 smoothest ]

>look

    英 [lʊk]  美 [lʊk]
    vt. 看；期待；注意；面向；看上去像
    vi. 看；看起来；注意；面向
    n. 看；样子；面容
    n. (Look)人名；(瑞典)洛克；(英)卢克
      look at sth看...（表示盯着一个东西..）
      look for寻找
      What are you looking for?你正在找什么？
      look out:小心
      look out of the window. (当句子中时,表示看.. 外面)看窗户的外面.

>watch

    英 [wɒtʃ]  美 [wɑtʃ]
    vt. 观察；注视；看守；警戒
    n. 手表；监视；守护；值班人
    vi. 观看，注视；守侯，看守
    [ 复数 watches 过去式 watched 过去分词 watched 现在分词 watching ]
    wacth 表示全神贯注的看一个东西
    wacth TV 看电视(固定搭配)
    see a movie 看电影(看电影的看要用see)（固定搭配）

>must

    英 [mʌst]  美 [mʌst]
    aux. 必须，一定；可以，应当；很可能
    n. 绝对必要的事物；未发酵葡萄汁
    n. (Must)人名；(匈)穆 什特；(俄、瑞典)穆斯特
    You should go.你应该走了
    You can go.你可以走了
    You must go.你必须走了

>call

    英 [kɔːl]  美 [kɔl]
    vi. 呼叫；拜访；叫牌
    vt. 呼叫；称呼；召集
    n. 电话；呼叫；要求；访问
    n. (Call)人名；(瑞典、罗)卡尔；(英)考尔
    1.叫，请
    Call me at 6 o'clock.呼叫我在6点钟
    2,n.电话
    Give me a call 给我一个电话。

>doctor

     英 ['dɒktə]  美 ['dɑktɚ]
     vt. 修理；篡改，伪造；为…治病；授以博士学位
     n. 医生；博士
     vi. 就医；行医
    在口语中常简化为doc

>telephone

    英 ['telɪfəʊn]  美 [ˈtɛləfon]
    n. （美）电话(座机)；电话机；电话耳机,
    vi. 打电话
    vt. 打电话给…
    [ 过去式 telephoned 过去分词 telephoned 现在分词 telephoning ]

>remember

    英 [rɪ'membə]  美 [rɪ'mɛmbɚ]
    vt. 记得；牢记；纪念；代…问好
    vi. 记得，记起
    1记得，记住
    used to.. 过去常常做某事.
    I remember he used to dress in a blue suit。我记得他过去常常穿一件蓝色的外套.
    2.记住，牢记，不忘记。
    Remember your appointmnet(约定) with the dentist(牙医).

>mouth

    英 [maʊθ]  美 [maʊθ]
    n. 口，嘴；河口
    vt. 做作地说，装腔作势地说；喃喃地说出
    vi. 装腔作势说话
    [ 复数 mouths ]

>twister

    英 ['twɪstə]  美 ['twɪstɚ]
    n. 缠绕者；不可靠的人；难题；旋转球；绕口令

>tongue

    英 [tʌŋ]  美 [tʌŋ]
    n. 舌头；语言
    vt. 舔；斥责；用舌吹
    vi. 说话；吹管乐器
    n. (Tongue)人名；(英)唐
    [ 过去式 tongued 过去分词 tongued 现在分词 tonguing ]
    tongue twister:绕口令
    mother tongue母语
    This guy has a dirty tongue.(这个人有一个脏的舌头，就表示这个认喜欢说脏话)
    Someone has a bitter(哭的) bongue某人有一个苦的舌头。就表示某人喜欢说一些尖酸刻薄的话.

>bad

    英 [bæd]  美 [bæd]
    adj. 坏的；严重的；劣质的
    n. 坏事；坏人
    adv. 很，非常；坏地；邪恶地
    n. (Bad)人名；(罗)巴德
    [ 比较级 worse 最高级 worst ]

>cold    .

    英 [kəʊld]  美 [kold]
    adj. 寒冷的；冷淡的，不热情的；失去知觉的
    n. 寒冷；感冒
    adv. 完全地
    [ 比较级 colder 最高级 coldest ]


######课文录音

    MR.WILLIAMS: Where's Jimmy?
    MRS.WILLIAMS: He's in bed.
    在床上，用in bed,而不是on bed.

    MR.WILLIAMS:What's the matter with him?
    他怎么了？
    What's the matter with... ... 怎么了？

    MRS.WILLIAMS:He feels ill.

    MR.WILLIAMS:He looks ill.
    MRS.WILLIAMS:We must call the doctor.
    MR.WILLIAMS:Yes,we must.
    MR.WILLIAMS:Can you remember the doctor's telephone number?
    MRS.WILLIAMS:Yes,It's 09754.
    DOCDOR:Open your mouth,Jimmy.Show me your tonuge.Say'Ah'.
    MR.WILLIAMS:What's the matter with him,doctor?
    DOCTOR:He has a bad cold,Mr.Williams,he must saty in bed for a week.
    MRS.WILLIAMS:That's good news for Jimmy.
    DOCTOR:Good news?Why?
    MR.WILLIAMS:Because he doesn't like school.

    He feels ill.
    主语+系动词+表语  结构

    系动词

     包括 1.be动词 +形容词/名词 （be动词后面可以加形容词或名词）

          This girl is beautiful.
          This is my school.

          2.感官动词 + 形容词 （感官动词后面可以加形容词）
          He feels ill.  他感觉生病了。
          I feel happy/sad. 我感觉开心.伤心.
          She loos sad.她看起来伤心的。
          This dish tastes good.这道菜尝起来好的。
          The food smells terrible.这个驶入闻起来可怕的.

      be动词 am/is/are
      感官动词 身体可以感受到的动作 。 闻，感受这样类型的用身体感受的词叫做感官动词


###### 口语快门

        说两种人

        owl
        英 [aʊl]  美 [aʊl]
        n. 猫头鹰；枭；惯于晚上活动的人

        night owl 夜猫子
        stay up熬夜
        ill
        英 [tɪl]  美 [tɪl]
        n. [地理][水文] 冰碛；放钱的抽屉；备用现金
        prep. 直到
        conj. 直到...为止
        vt. 耕种；犁
        vi. 耕种；耕耘
        n. (Till)人名；(法)蒂伊；(匈、德、捷)蒂尔；(英)蒂尔(女子教名Matilda的昵称)

        I always stay up late till 2 o'clock, 我总是熬夜到2点
        I am a night owl.我是一个夜猫子

        night person 爱熬夜的人
        night owl

        morning person 早起的人

### 62\. <a id="one-sixty-two">lesson  sixty-two What's the matter with them?What must the do?<a/>

######单词精讲

>head

    英 [hed]  美 [hɛd]
    n. 头；头痛；上端；最前的部分；理解力
    vt. 前进；用头顶；作为…的首领；站在…的前头；给…加标题
    vi. 出发；成头状物；船驶往
    adj. 头的；主要的；在顶端的
    n. (Head)人名；(英)黑德

>ache

    英 [eɪk]  美 [ek]
    vi. 疼痛；渴望
    n. 疼痛
    n. (Ache)人名；(德)阿赫；(西)阿切
    [ 过去式 ached 过去分词 ached 现在分词 aching ]

>headache

    英 ['hedeɪk]  美 [ˈhɛdˌek]

    vi. 忍受

>stomach ache

     英 [ˈstʌmək eɪk]  美 [ˈstʌmək eɪk]

     [ 复数 aspirin或aspirins

###### 书面练习

    A Rewrite these sentencves using He.

    Example:
    I have  a headache.
    I must stay at home.
    He has headache.
    He must stay at home.

    one.
    I have a cold.
    He has a cold.
    two
    I can't go to work.
    He can't go to work.
    three.
    I am not well.
    He is not well.
    four.
    I feel ill.
    He feels ill.
    five.
    I must see a doctor.
    He must see a doctor.
    six.
    I do not like doctors.
    He doesn't like doctors.

    B   Write sentences like these in the examle.

        Jimmy/(a stomach ache)/a headache/take an aspirin
        What's the matter with Jimmy?
        Does he have a stomach ache?
        No,he doesn't have a stomach ache.
        He has a headache.
        So he must take an sapirin.

        one.Elizabeth/(an earache)/a headache/take an aspirin
        What's the matter with Elizabeth？
        Does she have an earache?
        No,she doesn't have an earache.
        She sha a headache.
        So she must take an aspirin.

        two.George/(a headache)/an earache/see a doctor.
        What's the matter with George?
        Does he  have a headache?
        No,He doesn't have a headache.
        He has an earache.
        So he must see a doctor.

        three.Jim/(a stomach ache)/a toothache/see a dentist
        What's the matter with Jim?
        Does he have a stomach ache?
        No,he doesn't have a stomach ache.
        He has a toothache.
        So he must see a dentist.

        four.Jane/(a toothache)/a stomach ache/take some medicine
        What's the matter with Jane?
        Does she have a toothace?
        No,she doesn't have a toothace.
        She has a stomach ache.
        So she must take some medicine.

        five.Sam(a stomach ache)/a temperature/go to bed
        What's the matter with Sam?
        Does he have a stomach ache?
        No,he doesn't have a stomach ache.
        He has a temperature.
        So he must go to bed.

        six.Dave(a headache)/flu/stay in bed
        What's the matter wiht Dave?
        Does he have a headache?
        No,he doesn't have a headache.
        He has flu.(flu前不用接a或an)
        So he must stay in bed.

        seven.Jimmy(a headache)measles/we... call the doctor
        What's the matter with Jimmy?
        Does he have a headache?
        No,he doesn't has a headache.
        He has measles.
        So we must call the doctor.

        eight.Susan(an earache)/mumps/we....call the doctor
        What's the matter with  Susan?
        Does she have an earache?
        No,she doesn't have an earache.
        She has mumps.
        So we must call the doctor.

 ### 63\. <a id="one-sixty-three">lesson  sixty-three  Thank you,doctor.<a/>

######单词精讲

>better

    better
    英 ['betə]  美 ['bɛtɚ]
    n. 长辈；较好者；打赌的人（等于bettor）
    adv. 更好的；更多的；较大程度地
    adj. 较好的
    vt. 改善；胜过
    vi. 变得较好
    n. (Better)人名；(西、瑞典、德)贝特尔
    形容词well/good 的比较级
    beeter3个在英语中常用的短语
    Better late than never.汪洋补牢为时未晚
    Better safe than sorry.稳妥总比后悔好
    For better or for worse.不论好坏(同甘共苦)。
    I am your friend,so for better or for worse,I will always be with you,
    I will always be on your side.
    我是你的朋友，不论好坏，我都将与你在一起，我总是在你这一边。

> certainly

    英 [ˈsəːt(ə)nli]  美 ['sɝtnli]
    adv. 当然；行（用于回答）；必定

>get up

    起床


>wake up

    醒来

>yet

    et
    英 [jet]  美 [jɛt]
    adv. 还；但是；已经
    conj(连词). 但是；然而
    n. (Yet)人名；(东南亚国家华语)一
    yet更多用于否定句



>rich

    英 [rɪtʃ]  美 [rɪtʃ]
    adj. 富有的；肥沃的；昂贵的
    adj. 油腻的，含有很多脂肪
    n. (Rich)人名；(丹)里克；(捷)里赫；(英、西)里奇；(葡、法)里什
    反义词是pool

>remain

    英 [rɪ'meɪn]  美 [rɪ'men]
    vi. 保持；继续；依然；
    留下；停下；
    剩余；逗留；残存
    n. 遗迹；剩余物，残骸
    We're going to remain in Nanjing for another two days.
    我们将要在南京停留两天。
    It will remain cold for a couple of days.
    for a couple of days 表示还要几天
    天气将持续寒冷还要几天。
    Most people remain silent at the meeting.
    大多数的人在会议上都保持安静的.

###### 听录音

    DOCTOR: How's Jimmy today?

    MRS.WILLIAMS: Better,Thank you ,doctor.

    DOCTOR:Can I see him please,Mrs.Williams?

    MRS.WILLIAMS:Certainly,doctor.Come upstairs,
                      当然，医生，上楼吧.
    DOCTOR:      You look very well,Jimmy.
                  你看起来好的，吉米
                 You are better,but you mustn't get up yet.
                 你是更好的，但是你H还不能起床.
                 You must stay in bed for another two days.
                 你必须躺在床上另外两天。
    DOCTOR:      The boy mustn't go to school yet,Mrs.Williams.
                 And he mustn't eat rich food.
    MRS.WILLIAMS:Does he have a temperature,doctor？
    DOCTRO:       No,he doesn't.
    MRS.WILLIAMS: Must he stay in bed?
    DOCTOR:       Yes,He must remain in bed for  another two days.
                  He can get up for about two hours each day,
                  but you must keep the room warm.
    DOCTOR:       Where's Mr.williams this evening？
    MRS.WILLIAMS: He's in bed,doctor.
                  Can you see him please?
                  He has a bad cold,too!

###### 口语快门

    如果迷路了，有哪些句型可以问别人
    where
    Where is the 5th street?
    第五大街在哪里？
    Where am I on this map?
    我在哪里在这个地图上？
    Where am I located?
    我是坐落在哪里？
    how
    How do I get to the 5th street?
    我如何做能到达第五大街？


    Is it near here?
    它靠近这里吗？

    Is it within walking distance?
    它是在步行距离里吗？

    how far:多远
    How far is it to the 5th street?
    到达第五大街有多远？

    How long:多久
    How long will it take to get to the 5th street?
     还有多久他将到达第五大街？


    Which bus should I take to get here?
    我应该乘坐哪一辆公交车达到哪里？

    Which subway should I take to get here?
    我应该乘坐哪一辆地铁达到哪里？


    How much would the taxi cost to get here?
    出租车达到哪里可能花费多少钱？

    Kelly ClarKson
    Because of You
